(80, " To solve this problem, we need to use the concept of percentage change.\nLet's assume the original price of petroleum oil was $X per unit. After a 10.0% increase in price, the new price becomes $X + 10% of $X = $X + 0.1X = $X + $0.1X.\nNow, if the consumer reduces their oil consumption by the same percentage (10.0%), their new consumption is (1 - 0.10)X = 0.9X.\nTo find the new petroleum bill, we need to multiply the new consumption by the new price:\nNew petroleum bill = 0.9X x ($X + $0.1X) = 0.9X x $X + 0.9X x $0.1X\n= $0.9X^2 + $0.9X\nSo, the new petroleum bill would be $0.9X^2 + $0.9X.\nTherefore, the percentage change in the petroleum bill would be:\nPercentage change in petroleum bill = ($0.9X^2 + $0.9X - $X^2 - $X) / $X\n= $0.9X + $0.9 - $X - $0.9\n= $0.9X - $0.9\nSo, the petroleum bill would decrease by $0.9X.")

(154, " Great, let's calculate the simple interest earned on the deposit of $70 in a savings account with an annual interest rate of 3.0% over 2.5 years.\nStep 1: Determine the principal amount (P)\nThe principal amount is the initial deposit of $70.\nP = $70\n\nStep 2: Determine the time period (t)\nThe time period is the duration for which the interest is calculated, which is 2.5 years.\nt = 2.5 years = 25 months\n\nStep 3: Calculate the interest (I)\nThe interest is calculated by multiplying the principal amount (P) by the interest rate (r) for the time period (t).\nI = P x r x t\nI = $70 x 3.0% x 25 months\nI = $70 x 0.03 x 25 = $750\n\nStep 4: Calculate the total amount (A)\nThe total amount is the principal amount plus the interest earned.\nA = P + I\nA = $70 + $750\nA = $820\n\nTherefore, the simple interest earned on a deposit of $70 in a savings account with an annual interest rate of 3.0% over 2.5 years is $820.")

(646, " Great, let's dive into this problem! To find out how much money Olivia would have made, we need to use the information given in the problem.\n1. Each chocolate bar costs $3.00.\n2. A box has 7.0 bars in total.\n3. Olivia sold all but 4.0 bars.\n\nLet's represent the information in a diagram:\n\n$$ \\begin{array}{ccc} \\text{Number of chocolate bars} & \\text{Cost per bar} & \\text{Total cost} \\\\ \\hline 7.0 & 3.00 & 21.00 \\\\ \\hline \\text{Olivia sold} & & 3.00 \\\\ \\hline \\text{Remaining bars} & & 4.00 \\\\ \\hline \\end{array} $$\nNow, let's find out how much money Olivia would have made by selling the chocolate bars:\n$$ \\text{Total cost} = 21.00 $$\n$$ \\text{Total money made} = \\text{Total cost} - \\text{Cost per bar} \\times \\text{Number of bars sold} $$\n$$ \\text{Total money made} = 21.00 - 3.00 \\times 3 = 17.00 $$\nTherefore, Olivia would have made $17.00 by selling all but 4 chocolate bars from a box that contains 7 bars and each bar costs $3.00.")
